				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Herr, deine Augen sehen nach dem Glauben, BWV 102 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (7 movements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Herr, deine Augen sehen nach dem Glauben
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Lord, Your eyes look for faith!
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Herr</span>; <span title="he">Herr, deine Augen sehen nach dem Glauben, רי"ב 102</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/185143506">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herr,_deine_Augen_sehen_nach_dem_Glauben,_BWV_102">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/185143506">185143506</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n88045323">n88045323</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300007949">300007949</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13925794v">13925794v</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 102&#160;; BC A 119
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 283
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>G minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (7 movements):
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte prima
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Chorus: Herr, deine Augen sehen nach dem Glauben (G&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>2. Recitativo (Bass): Wo ist das Ebenbild, das Gott (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd><dd>3. Aria (Alto): Weh der Seele, die den Schaden (F&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>4. Arioso (Bass): Verachtest du den Reichtum seiner (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte seconda
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>5. Aria (Tenor): Erschrecke doch (G&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>6. Recitativo (Alto): Bei Warten ist Gefahr (C&#160;minor)-G&#160;major)
</dd><dd>7. Chorale: Heut lebst du, heut bekehre dich (C&#160;minor)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1726-08-25 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1830 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd>Jeremiah 5: 3 (No.1)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Anonymous" title="Category:Anonymous">Anonymous</a> (Nos.2-3, 5-6)<br />Romans 2: 4-5 (No.4)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Heermann,_Johann" title="Category:Heermann, Johann">Johann Heermann</a> (1585-1647) (No.7)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> alto, tenor, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> flute traverso (or violin piccolo), 2 oboes, strings, continuo (organ)
